      "# np.histogram returns the bin edges, so there will be 50 probability\n",

      "%%file fibonacci.py\n",
      "def fibonacci(x):\n",
      "    a = 1\n",
      "    b = 1\n",
      "    i = 1\n",
      "    while i <= x:\n",
      "        if i == 1 or i == 2:\n",
      "            yield 1\n",
      "        else:\n",
      "            result = a + b\n",
      "            yield result\n",
      "            a = b\n",
      "            b = result\n",
      "        i += 1\n",
      "\n",
      "if __name__ == '__main__':\n",
      "    fibo = [i for i in fibonacci(10)]"
